<h1 class="firstHeading mw-first-heading" id="firstHeading"><span class="mw-page-title-main">Milk Bucket</span></h1>
<div class="vector-body" id="bodyContent">
<div class="noprint" id="siteSub">From Minecraft Wiki</div>
<div id="contentSub"><span class="mw-redirectedfrom">(Redirected from <a class="mw-redirect" href="/w/Bucket_of_Milk?redirect=no" title="Bucket of Milk">Bucket of Milk</a>)</span></div>
<div id="contentSub2"></div>
<div id="jump-to-nav"></div>

<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#searchInput">Jump to search</a>

<p>A <b>milk bucket</b> (in <a href="/w/Java_Edition" title="Java Edition"><i>Java Edition</i></a>) or <b>milk</b> (in <a href="/w/Bedrock_Edition" title="Bedrock Edition"><i>Bedrock Edition</i></a>). is a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/w/Drink" title="Drink">drink</a> obtained from <span class="explain" title="Defaults to right click on mouse or left trigger on gamepad.">using</span> a <a href="/w/Bucket" title="Bucket">bucket</a> on <a href="/w/Cow" title="Cow">cows</a>, <a href="/w/Mooshroom" title="Mooshroom">mooshrooms</a> and <a href="/w/Goat" title="Goat">goats</a> that can be consumed to clear all <a href="/w/Effect" title="Effect">effects</a>.
</p>
<div aria-labelledby="mw-toc-heading" class="toc" id="toc" role="navigation"><input class="toctogglecheckbox" id="toctogglecheckbox" role="button" style="display:none" type="checkbox"/><div class="toctitle" dir="ltr" lang="en"><h2 id="mw-toc-heading">Contents</h2><span class="toctogglespan"><label class="toctogglelabel" for="toctogglecheckbox"></label></span></div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Obtaining">Obtaining</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="/w/Milk_Bucket?section=1&amp;veaction=edit" title="Edit section: Obtaining">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Milk_Bucket?action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Obtaining">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Harvesting">Harvesting</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="/w/Milk_Bucket?section=2&amp;veaction=edit" title="Edit section: Harvesting">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Milk_Bucket?action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Harvesting">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Milk buckets can be obtained from <a href="/w/Cow" title="Cow">cows</a>, <a href="/w/Mooshroom" title="Mooshroom">mooshrooms</a>, and <a href="/w/Goat" title="Goat">goats</a> by pressing <span class="explain" title="Defaults to right click on mouse or left trigger on gamepad.">use</span> while looking at them with an empty <a href="/w/Bucket" title="Bucket">bucket</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Mob_loot">Mob loot</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="/w/Milk_Bucket?section=3&amp;veaction=edit" title="Edit section: Mob loot">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Milk_Bucket?action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Mob loot">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>A milk bucket has a chance of dropping from a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/w/Wandering_trader" title="Wandering trader">wandering trader</a>, if the trader is killed while holding it.‌<sup class="noprint nowrap Inline-Template" title="">[<i><span title="This statement only applies to Java Edition"><a href="/w/Java_Edition" title="Java Edition">Java Edition</a>  only</span></i>]</sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage">Usage</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="/w/Milk_Bucket?section=4&amp;veaction=edit" title="Edit section: Usage">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Milk_Bucket?action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Usage">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Holding <span class="explain" title="Defaults to right click on mouse or left trigger on gamepad.">use</span> with a milk bucket starts the drinking sound and animation. In <a href="/w/Java_Edition" title="Java Edition"><i>Java Edition</i></a>, the animation is shown only in first-person camera mode.
</p><p>When consumed, milk immediately removes all status <a href="/w/Effect" title="Effect">effects</a> from the <a href="/w/Player" title="Player">player</a>. <a href="/w/Fire" title="Fire">Fire</a> is not a status effect; therefore, drinking milk doesn't extinguish a burning player.
</p><p>The benefits of area status effects granted by <a href="/w/Beacon" title="Beacon">beacons</a> and <a href="/w/Conduit_Power" title="Conduit Power">conduit power</a> are restored almost immediately in Bedrock Edition and after a few seconds in <i>Java Edition</i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Crafting_ingredient">Crafting ingredient</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="/w/Milk_Bucket?section=5&amp;veaction=edit" title="Edit section: Crafting ingredient">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Milk_Bucket?action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Crafting ingredient">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

</td>
<td>Empty <a href="/w/Bucket" title="Bucket">buckets</a> remain in the crafting grid after crafting the cake.
</td></tr>
</tbody></table>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="/w/Milk_Bucket?section=12&amp;veaction=edit" title="Edit section: History">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Milk_Bucket?action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: History">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<table class="wikitable" data-description="History" style="image-rendering: pixelated;"><tbody><tr><th colspan="6"><a href="/w/Java_Edition_Alpha" title="Java Edition Alpha">Java Edition Alpha</a></th></tr>
<tr><th class="nowrap" colspan="5" rowspan="1"><a href="/w/Java_Edition_Alpha_v1.0.8" title="Java Edition Alpha v1.0.8">v1.0.8</a></th><td><a class="image" href="/w/File:Milk_Bucket_JE1_BE1.png"><img alt="Milk Bucket JE1 BE1.png" data-file-height="160" data-file-width="160" decoding="async" height="32" loading="lazy" src="/images/thumb/Milk_Bucket_JE1_BE1.png/32px-Milk_Bucket_JE1_BE1.png?2ed5e" srcset="/images/thumb/Milk_Bucket_JE1_BE1.png/64px-Milk_Bucket_JE1_BE1.png?2ed5e 2x" width="32"/></a> Milk has been introduced, but it has no purpose and is obtainable only through inventory editing.
<pre class="history-json noexcerpt navigation-not-searchable">{"type": "java Alpha", "version": "v1.0.8",  "content": "(link to File:Milk Bucket JE1 BE1.png article, displayed as 32px) Milk has been introduced, but it has no purpose and is obtainable only through inventory editing."}</pre></td></tr>
<tr><th class="nowrap" colspan="5" rowspan="1"><a href="/w/Java_Edition_Alpha_v1.0.11" title="Java Edition Alpha v1.0.11">v1.0.11</a></th><td>Milk can now be obtained by <span class="explain" title="Defaults to right click on mouse or left trigger on gamepad.">milking</span> a <a href="/w/Cow" title="Cow">cow</a> with a <a href="/w/Bucket" title="Bucket">bucket</a>. However, it is not yet drinkable.
<pre class="history-json noexcerpt navigation-not-searchable">{"type": "java Alpha", "version": "v1.0.11",  "content": "Milk can now be obtained by &lt;span  class=\"explain \" title=\"Defaults to right click on mouse or left trigger on gamepad.\"&gt;milking&lt;/span&gt; a (link to cow article, displayed as cow) with a (link to bucket article, displayed as bucket). However, it is not yet drinkable."}</pre></td></tr>
